      <article class="post-572 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail category-diy-and-crafts category-home category-vintage tag-diy-projects tag-vintage-in-the-home entry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
       <header class="entry-header">
        <h1 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline">
         How To Update A Vintage Enamel Top Table
        </h1>
        <p class="entry-meta">
         <time class="entry-time" datetime="2011-02-26T10:13:00+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">
          February 26, 2011
         </time>
         by
         <span class="entry-author" itemprop="author" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
          <a class="entry-author-link" href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/author/pamhouseofhawthornes-com/" itemprop="url" rel="author">
           <span class="entry-author-name" itemprop="name">
            Pam
           </span>
          </a>
         </span>
         <span class="entry-comments-link">
          <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/vintage-enamel-top-table-part-2-or-mr/#comments">
           48 Comments
          </a>
         </span>
        </p>
       </header>
       <div class="entry-content" itemprop="text">
        <p>
         If you missed installment number one of Mr. Chippy you can read about me rescuing my mothers
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/vintage-enamel-top-table/" target="_blank">
          vintage enamel topped table
         </a>
         . He wasnt being held hostage or anything, he had just been a little mistreated and neglected.
        </p>
        <p>
         He now resides happily at my house.
        </p>
        <p>
         This is what he started as
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-1.jpg">
          <img alt="A DIY project with heart.  How I rescued and updated my mom's vintage enamel topped table.  It looked pretty grungy BEFORE, but the AFTER looks so much better :) " class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-10072 pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-1.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/vintage-enamel-top-table-part-2-or-mr/" height="510" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-1.jpg" width="680"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         and what he looks like now.
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-10.jpg">
          <img alt="A DIY project with heart.  How I rescued and updated my mom's vintage enamel topped table.  It looked pretty grungy BEFORE, but the AFTER looks so much better :) " class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-10073 pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-10.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/vintage-enamel-top-table-part-2-or-mr/" height="510" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-10.jpg" width="680"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         I solved the excessive chippiness and rust problem by unscrewing the enamel top and turning it around 180 degrees.
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-19.jpg">
          <img alt="A DIY project with heart.  How I rescued and updated my mom's vintage enamel topped table.  It looked pretty grungy BEFORE, but the AFTER looks so much better :) " class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-10074 pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-19.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/vintage-enamel-top-table-part-2-or-mr/" height="510" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-19.jpg" width="680"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         I know that doesnt
         <em>
          really
         </em>
         solve the problem, but it is a heck of a lot less noticeable now, since I can put the bad spot against a wall.
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-18.jpg">
          <img alt="A DIY project with heart.  How I rescued and updated my mom's vintage enamel topped table.  It looked pretty grungy BEFORE, but the AFTER looks so much better :) " class="aligncenter wp-image-10075 size-large pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-18.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/vintage-enamel-top-table-part-2-or-mr/" height="510" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-18-680x510.jpg" width="680"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         Using soap and water and spray cleaners really didnt even TOUCHthe embedded black stuff on the top, so I brought outmy trusty Bar Keepers Friend and it got the majority of the 100 years of dirt off of it.
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-20.jpg">
          <img alt="A DIY project with heart.  How I rescued and updated my mom's vintage enamel topped table.  It looked pretty grungy BEFORE, but the AFTER looks so much better :) " class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-10076 pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-20.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/vintage-enamel-top-table-part-2-or-mr/" height="510" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-20.jpg" width="680"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         If youve never used it,
         <a href="http://www.barkeepersfriend.com/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.barkeepersfriend.com/', 'Bar Keepers Friend ');">
          Bar Keepers Friend
         </a>
         is like Comet Cleanser except not gritty and it doesnt scratch. I originally bought it to keep my fancy cookware looking shiny, but I am finding more and more places to use it.
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-15.jpg">
          <img alt="A DIY project with heart.  How I rescued and updated my mom's vintage enamel topped table.  It looked pretty grungy BEFORE, but the AFTER looks so much better :) " class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-10077 pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-15.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/vintage-enamel-top-table-part-2-or-mr/" height="510" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-15.jpg" width="680"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         This is one of my favorite kitchen towels, although I never actually use it for dishes. Dont we all have just-for-look towels?
        </p>
        <p>
         Its not just me is it?
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-11.jpg">
          <img alt="A DIY project with heart.  How I rescued and updated my mom's vintage enamel topped table.  It looked pretty grungy BEFORE, but the AFTER looks so much better :) " class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-10078 pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-11.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/vintage-enamel-top-table-part-2-or-mr/" height="510" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-11.jpg" width="680"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-12.jpg">
          <img alt="A DIY project with heart.  How I rescued and updated my mom's vintage enamel topped table.  It looked pretty grungy BEFORE, but the AFTER looks so much better :) " class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-10079 pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-12.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/vintage-enamel-top-table-part-2-or-mr/" height="510" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-12.jpg" width="680"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         One of my favorite mixing bowls with my vintage egg beater.
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-13.jpg">
          <img alt="A DIY project with heart.  How I rescued and updated my mom's vintage enamel topped table.  It looked pretty grungy BEFORE, but the AFTER looks so much better :) " class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-10080 pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-13.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/vintage-enamel-top-table-part-2-or-mr/" height="510" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-13.jpg" width="680"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         You didnt think I was actually mixing something up in here, did you? Nope, just for looks.
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-14.jpg">
          <img alt="A DIY project with heart.  How I rescued and updated my mom's vintage enamel topped table.  It looked pretty grungy BEFORE, but the AFTER looks so much better :) " class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-10081 pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-14.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/vintage-enamel-top-table-part-2-or-mr/" height="510" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-14.jpg" width="680"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         I cleaned the paint off the original handle with a wire brush on my husbands bench grinder. Its that machine with all the stiff twirling metal wires that looks like it could take your fingers off if you slipped.
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-16.jpg">
          <img alt="A DIY project with heart.  How I rescued and updated my mom's vintage enamel topped table.  It looked pretty grungy BEFORE, but the AFTER looks so much better :) " class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-10082 pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-16.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/vintage-enamel-top-table-part-2-or-mr/" height="510" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-16.jpg" width="680"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         And the paint sort of fell off the label while I was taking it off the table. Sort of like. magic. Then I just polished it up with the Bar Keepers Friend.
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-17.jpg">
          <img alt="A DIY project with heart.  How I rescued and updated my mom's vintage enamel topped table.  It looked pretty grungy BEFORE, but the AFTER looks so much better :) " class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-10083 pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-17.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/vintage-enamel-top-table-part-2-or-mr/" height="510" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table-17.jpg" width="680"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         The color used was Benjamin Moores Azores, but mixed at Home Depot in their semi-gloss Behr paint. I have nothing against Benjamin Moore paint, I just happened to be at Home Depot that day.
        </p>
        <p>
         Some of my photos make it look a little like 1980s country blue, but it is actually a turquoise/blue/green/gray color.
        </p>
        <p>
         One more look at Mr. Chippys before and after.
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table.jpg">
          <img alt="A DIY project with heart.  How I rescued and updated my mom's vintage enamel topped table.  It looked pretty grungy BEFORE, but the AFTER looks so much better :) " class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-10071 pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/vintage-enamel-top-table-part-2-or-mr/" height="1398" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/02/Enamel-Porcelain-Table.jpg" width="680"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <center>
         <a data-pin-color="red" data-pin-config="none" data-pin-do="buttonPin" data-pin-height="28" href="//www.pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.houseofhawthornes.com%2Fvintage-enamel-top-table-part-2-or-mr%2F&amp;media=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.houseofhawthornes.com%2Fwp-content%2Fuploads%2F2011%2F02%2FEnamel-Porcelain-Table.jpg&amp;description=A%20DIY%20project%20with%20heart.%20%20How%20I%20rescued%20and%20updated%20my%20mom's%20vintage%20enamel%20topped%20table.%20%20It%20looked%20pretty%20grungy%20BEFORE%2C%20but%20the%20AFTER%20looks%20so%20much%20better%20%3A)%20">
          <img alt="" class="pib-hover-img" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/vintage-enamel-top-table-part-2-or-mr/" src="//assets.pinterest.com/images/pidgets/pinit_fg_en_rect_red_28.png"/>
         </a>
         <br/>
         <!-- Please call pinit.js only once per page -->

         </script>
        </center>
        Hopefully hell last another few decades.
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.mylivesignature.com/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.mylivesignature.com/', '');" target="_blank">

         </a>
        </p>

           <p>
            We had this table when I was a child (Im 68 now) and when my mother passed away I moved this table to my new place. It had been in the basement for years. When I was having repairs done on my home the workers used it to set things on under the carport but decided to protect it they put a rubber backed rug on top of it. After all was said and done it got wet and dried over and over. Now there is the backing stuck to the top of it and I cant get it off. I was going to take it to car painting shop to have them fill a large chipped area (about 3) and then sand and spray it. Need to refinish but I dont know if that is the place to have it done. Any recommendations for a better place?
           </p>

I also have a Sno White table, found along the side of the road!  I have debated about painting ours.  The enamel on ours is in very good condition, the paint just a little flaky.
             </p>
